< username>
Michael T</username>
< review>
The whiners here are reflecting the decline of driving skills as of late.

I have been using the toll roads for over 4 years now, a couple times per week. I've never had an issue. Once I forgot to take my FasTrak, and didn't know it hadn't charged my account. Left the bill sitting for a bit, got notice of a violation and when I went to pay it, it was waived since it was my first violation.

- Don't go on your trip willy nilly. Look at your GPS before you leave and try to understand where you need to go. Use "Avoid Toll Roads" on Google Maps.
- You get plenty of time to pay your bill before it becomes a violation.
- Your first violation will be waived automatically.
- There are maps and toll calculators on their website.
- The rates rarely change and not by much, you'll get notified by email if you have an account or sign up for their newsletter.
- 90% of the rates fluctuate only a few cents throughout the day.
- I receive rate notices via email because I have an account on their website.

If you can't afford to use the toll road, then don't use them!

If you've realized you accidentally went on the toll road, it's your fault! Pay on the website.

If you didn't know you were on a toll road, read the signs!

Don't know where or how you're supposed to pay? Read the signs!

Need to update your information? Do it online and check to make sure it saved!

Have a FastTrak and getting billed recurrently? It's in the agreement. READ IT.

...Granted there are a couple people in these 100 reviews that have a legitimate complaint.< /review>

On 8/15/2020 I went to the Jiffy Lube on 3497 Stevens Creek Blvd in San Jose to receive an oil change. While I was waiting for service, one of the employees mentioned that my differential fluid was low and asked if I would like it "topped off." There was no mention of additional costs or fees, nor that it would require additional servicing beyond what is provided in the basic oil change. I agreed to having the fluid topped off. However, when it came to paying for what I thought was just an oil change for about $40, instead I was greeted with a bill for $140. I was charged an additional $100 for a complete flushing of my vehicles rear differential. I am furious that the service cost was not discussed with me before hand and the fact that I did NOT agree to a complete flushing of my vehicles rear differential. <gmapID>0x80c2bbbe07681355:0xe29110c4fc09216f<//gmapID>< Review>
I've been coming here for a couple of years now, and I noticed a lot of the reviews are a bit unfair. You come here for a traditional Thai massage, like you would actually get in Thailand. The masseuses are even all from Thailand. I've had my fair share of Thai massages in Thailand; from the decor, to the setup of the rooms, to the actual massages, it's a really authentic experience to what you'll get in Thailand.

Thai massage therapists are there to really work you over and beat you into submission. If you've got knots or any body soreness, they will ruthlessly attack it. Might be a little (or a lot) painful during, but you leave feeling loose. This includes using their feet and body weight to really loosen the muscles. And as with all traditional Thai massages, you lay on a cushion on the floor, rather than a table.

PSA - it's a cash-only establishment. They has free parking which is a great perk in LA these days!<//Review>

< review>
This place is super nondescript and looks how you'd expect for a basic massage/spa place. I only went here because I got a gift certificate for my birthday but I sure am glad I did! I made an appointment online but realized I was going to be about 15 minutes late (poor planning). I gave them a call letting them know and they were able to accommodate me no problem! I was helped almost right away after ringing the little bell on the counter and offered water.

The room itself was nice and clean and had a large cubby for me to store my clothes and things. My only complaint is that the rooms aren't fully closed off - the walls stop about 1-2 feet from the ceiling and the doors are sliding doors so you can hear the people next to you if they're talking/moving a lot. When I went there happened to be an older man that was making more noise than totally necessary. I get that you're enjoying your massage sir, but I 100% don't need to hear it. Amy had some soft music playing though so I was able to focus on that and relax.

The massage itself was AMAZING. I got a 60-minute combo Thai/Deep Tissue and I've never felt so great after a massage. I have scoliosis and carry a lot of tension in my traps and between my shoulder blades that can be hard to get to. She somehow cracked my entire spine by doing this move at the end where she put her knees in my back and bent me backwards. I have no idea how she is so strong but it was insane and I've never had my back cracked that fully before.

Love that they have an Early Bird special for massages booked earlier in the day! Just be sure to bring cash since it is CASH ONLY. Will be back!<//review>

<Time>1478045160185</Time><rating>5</rating>< Text>
My husband brought me here on our wedding anniversary for a couples massage (yay!). The whole experience was amazing! We had Patti and Gigi work on us, and we both felt relief from some incredibly tight spots/ knots that we had. We both circled "medium" pressure on our intake form. I would say their version of "medium" might be too intense for some folks, but it hit the spot for us (i.e. if you are newer to massage, or very sensitive to touch, I would recommend circling the "light" option). Also, when there was an area that was too tight or tender, the girls could sense that, and adjusted what they were doing to match where our body was. Overall a great find, and we will be back. One note/suggestion: if there is a way to soundproof the rooms more, that would be awesome. There is a dance studio next door, and we could here that music at times during our massage. Definitely a little distracting to hear dance music when getting a massage. Overall very happy with our experience!</Text>

The security gate restricted, one lane windy driveway up a hill provides the one way in and one way out.  I thought it would be difficult to deal with at first but it's not at all.  It simply makes it pretty and I feel an increased sense of security with it tucked away like it is, plus it's next door to a police station!.  Prices are the cheapest I've found at $55 for a small room!
